                s.parentNode.insertBefore(g, s);
            }(document, 'script'));
        </script>

                The team was known as the Chicago Black Hawks before 1986.<br><br>

<b>2015 Stanley Cup Championship Lineup</b><br>
Patrick Sharp - Jonathan Toews - Marian Hossa <br>
Brandon Saad - Brad Richards - Patrick Kane<br>
Kris Versteeg - Antonie Vermette - Teuvo Teräväinen<br>

Duncan Keith - Niklas Hjalmarsson<br>
Johnny Oduya  - Brent Seabrook<br>
Kimmo Timonen - Trevor Van Riemsdyk<br><br>

Cory Crawford<br>
(Scott Darling)<br><br>

Bryan Bickell - Jonathan Toews - Patrick Kane <br>
Patrick Sharp - Michal Handzus - Marián Hossa<br>
Brandon Saad - Andrew Shaw - Viktor Stålberg<br>
Marcus Krüger - Dave Bolland - Michael Frolík <br>
<br>
Duncan Keith - Brent Seabrook<br>
Johnny Oduya  - Niklas Hjalmarsson<br>

Cory Crawford<br>
(Ray Emery)<br>
